句式结构：No... nor...；neither… nor…；not… nor… </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: 话语</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">plea n. 请求；恳求；借口；托词</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She made an impassioned <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">plea</span></em></strong> for help.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她恳切地<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">求</strong>助。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He refused the appointment on a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">plea</span></em></strong> of illness.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">称</strong>病拒绝了那次约会。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. youth (the youth)</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英释：young people considered as a group （统称）青年，年轻人</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the nation's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">youth</span></em></strong> 全国<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">青年</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">the youth</span></em></strong> of today 当代<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">青年</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">youth</span></em></strong> unemployment <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">青年</strong>失业问题</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6240741" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfVOd2A2fQpsTu134F3K6BKdmUnWOTWvuvIvqFlVkzicFZKz0FYB5FNsD8piaMf9q1GkskqYMOxamZw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. it's what the teachers are themselves</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> (that can teach our youth what they should be). </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">唯有老师本人的为人，能够告诉我们的下一代应该成为什么样的人。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">反身代词 themselves 在句中用于强调，用来加强 the teachers 的语气，可译成“亲自”、“本人”。此时，它在句中作同位语。即使去掉，也不影响句子的完整性。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You must do it <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em border-box;">你必须<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自己</strong>做。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><g data-type="png?x-oss-process=style/xmorient" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This kind of theory of learning stuff. So let's just set an example for learning Chinese. What is your level now? Are you fluent talking in Chinese? Can you understand people talking in Chinese just in normal conversation?</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I would say partially. Sometimes I still don't understand. Sometimes I don't know how to express stuff, still. I’m only about two years in, but I still practice every day. It’s also slowed me down quite a bit that I’m learning to read and write it as well. I'm not just trying to orally be able to speak it. So it slows me down quite a bit. But it’s challenging. So it’s fun for me. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I use the method of immersion (沉浸式). Immersion means to surround yourself with something pretty much. What I do is I just keep it around me. Like I play music, TV shows, movies; I listen about podcast, I read articles, I talk to natives, I watch videos. I have an app that I play on. I started to try to read The Hunger Games (《饥饿游戏》), the Chinese version, but it was a little too hard. So I backed out for right now. I also have a Chinese dictionary, and sometimes I will just sit down and try to write in it and study that way. I’m always constantly asking natives if I’m right though. That seems like the most important thing. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section See that's partly the problem. I’m missing words here and there. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdTwhzcsDRO7kQAiaw7r18zmR10UGkhWHGWuPPuY0kjbOtjJIMtAonRje25tlfGzx4eI1aO04RaYqA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/icUbkq0ficEL643phLhiaQNnvyaGsH9iaS4tclWcCN1zTa3JlWjCcPmGsJFm4j5Zly1w9Qd6q3fT6j25cV8BeosN0A/640?wx_fmt=png?x-oss-process=style/xmorient" data-type="png?x-oss-process=style/xmorient" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's pretty good already because you're just learning all by yourself. I heard from a study, actually, just a couple of days ago that learning a second language or multiple languages <a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653524506&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=6159d541473d91c4ffad9ebaf8e9fd61&amp;chksm=f7e852d7c09fdbc1d5bcb12088e4e3bf75aac581c6ee49a9aae932e7ddede5a82cd4cf3815dd&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" target="_blank">help your brain to develop</a>. Not really IQly-developed, but actually develops your multi-tasking skills and definitely helps with your brain. So that is the merits of learning a second language. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why are you all of a sudden interested in learning Chinese? Why not Spanish or French, some other languages? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">That's a good question. I really I didn't know about that. That's pretty cool. The reason why I started to learn Chinese was because about two and a half years ago, I heard a theory that each language carries its own perception of the world. And that intrigued me. It felt like, well, I can only know things through direct experience. And this is so important because I’m so focused on self--growth. That was that's why it was so intriguing to me like really I can change my perception by learning a language. That's incredible. So I took a couple of weeks and picked a language in order to test the theory. I decided on Chinese because it was the complete opposite of my own language and I felt like that was the best to learn if a language could really change your perception. It is a tonal language which is completely opposite of my own and it is also by characters, instead of words or letters. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Sure, I almost picked Japanese, but there were too many good reasons to learn Chinese instead of Japanese because really that would have just been an excuse to watch anime (日本动画片). At the same time, I always really admired the Chinese culture. As a matter of fact, when I was in primary school, my teacher one time asked us to do a project on compare and contrast, we could pick anything that we wanted. I have always really been into other cultures. But at this time, I think I was fourteen fifteen. Anyway, I did the report on China and Japan and to compare the two to see what…just as so I could see which one I like better. <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I eventually did pick China as the one that I like better.</span></em></p></section></section><section style="height: 30px;border-bottom-width: 5px;border-bottom-style: solid;display: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.obvious  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [ˈɒbviəs]  美 [ˈɑːbviəs] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 明显的；显著的；平淡无奇的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Obvious effect 效果明显 ; 明显的效应</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">obvious unjust 显失公平</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The reason is blindingly obvious. 原因十分明显。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.identical </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [aɪˈdentɪkl]  美 [aɪˈdentɪkl] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 同一的；完全相同的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 完全相同的事物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an identical equation 恒等式</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be identical with 和完全相同 ; 与……一致 ; 与 ; 与……相同</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be identical 吻合</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.stroke  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [strəʊk]  美 [stroʊk]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. （游泳或划船的）划；中风；（打、击等的）一下；冲程；（成功的）举动；尝试；轻抚</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. （用笔等）画；轻抚；轻挪；敲击；划尾桨；划掉；（打字时）击打键盘</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 击球；作尾桨手，指挥划桨；（打字时）击打键盘</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He had a minor stroke in 1987, which left him partly paralysed.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他在1987年患了轻度中风，这使他半身不遂了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.be unaware of 不知道；没有察觉到</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义：不知道；没有察觉到have no idea, wonder if</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He seemed to be unaware of the trouble he was causing. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他似乎还没有警觉到到自己惹起的麻烦。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.discern  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [dɪˈsɜːn]  美 [dɪˈsɜːrn]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 觉察出；识别；了解；隐约看见</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 辨别</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Discern Location 感知位置 ; 辨位术</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Discern Lies 辨识谎言 ; 洞悉谎言 ; 识破谎言</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">discern safely 安全识别</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义：vt. 识别；领悟，认识recognize , identify</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 看清楚，辨别see clearly, tell from</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The adult observers were able to reliably discern an assortment of emotions on the babies' faces. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">成年观察者能够有依据地辨别出婴儿脸上的各种情绪。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.duck </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [dʌk]  美 [dʌk] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 鸭子；鸭肉；（英）宝贝儿；零分</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 闪避；没入水中</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 躲避；猛按…入水</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. (Duck)人名；(德、葡、匈)杜克</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hans deftly ducked their blows.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉斯灵活地躲过了他们的猛击。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He ducked his head to hide his admiration.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他低下头以掩饰他的羡慕。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">P.S.</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: "Do not dream of treachery. My eyes can see through walls and into the minds of men. They will be on you wherever you go. At the first sign of disobedience I will lay such spells on you that anything you sit down on will feel like red hot iron and whenever you lie in a bed there will be invisible blocks of ice at your feet. Now go."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他刚走到门口，女巫说，“站住，别想耍花招。我的眼睛可以穿透墙壁，看到人的内心。你走到哪儿都逃不出我的眼睛。只要你再出不服从我的苗头，我就会诅咒你，你坐的任何东西都会像烧红的铁，任何时候你躺上床，脚下朝会有看不见的冰块。现在走吧。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 联络到你弟弟了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 还没有，我好担心。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 报警太蠢了吧，他大概只是在哪里过夜而已。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 或许你是对的。不过我还是担心。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: So did you get in touch with your brother? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, not yet. I'm really worried. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, it'd be foolish to call the police. He probably just went away overnight. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Maybe you're right. with some friends.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">M</strong>: Text me the address, and I'll see you there.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, rgb(223, 248, 255) 0%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 50%, rgb(253, 222, 219) 50%, rgb(253, 222, 219) 100%);padding: 5px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 17px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);letter-spacing: 4px;line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px;text-shadow: rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px -1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px -1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px 0px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 0px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px 0px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 0px -1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">情境分析</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 10px;border-width: 0px;background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgb(253, 222, 219) 0%, rgb(253, 222, 219) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Emily想要约著名的设计师皮尔卡丹谈工作的事情，便向皮尔卡丹的侄子马修致电邀约。结果，马修说他的舅舅最近为了时装周忙得不可开交，不得空。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgb(253, 222, 219) 0%, rgb(253, 222, 219) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 100%);padding: 5px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 17px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);letter-spacing: 4px;line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px;text-shadow: rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px -1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px -1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 1px 0px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 0px 1px, rgb(127, 127, 127) -1px 0px, rgb(127, 127, 127) 0px -1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 10px;border-width: 0px;background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgb(253, 222, 219) 0%, rgb(253, 222, 219) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 50%, rgb(223, 248, 255) 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家找到今天的主题词链了吗？那就是：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">work nonstop with XX 为了XX忙得不可开交；忙得焦头乱额；忙得团团转</strong></em></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，以后说到“忙”我们不要只用busy啦，我们可以用上今天学习的词链啦。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My mom is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">working nonstop with </strong>the dinner tonight. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">妈妈为了今天的晚餐<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All the waiters are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">working nonstop with </strong>the Party so close.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有服务生为了要开始的聚会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">关于“忙”还可以怎么说呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep XX occupied  XX忙得团团转</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be kept occupied </strong>when kids on holidays. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子们一放假，我的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">行程就是满满的</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be overwhelmed  很忙乱</span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">if you had done what I asked you to do this morning, then I wouldn't have<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> been overwhelmed</strong> and I would have remembered my wallet.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">早上你要是按我说的做了，我就不会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得团团转</strong>，也不会把钱包落家里了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be crazy busy 忙疯了</span></strong></span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">been crazy busy</strong> these last few days!</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最近几天她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>！</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 1.8;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词链可以用在礼貌地提出自己的需求时。</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I was wondering if</strong> I could take you on a date.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tom said he would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">come by to</strong> grab a bite.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tom说他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">要来</strong>吃点东西。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家找到今天的主题词链了吗？那就是：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">work nonstop with XX 为了XX忙得不可开交；忙得焦头乱额；忙得团团转</strong></em></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，以后说到“忙”我们不要只用busy啦，我们可以用上今天学习的词链啦。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My mom is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">working nonstop with </strong>the dinner tonight. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">妈妈为了今天的晚餐<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All the waiters are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">working nonstop with </strong>the Party so close.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有服务生为了要开始的聚会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">关于“忙”还可以怎么说呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep XX occupied  XX忙得团团转</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be kept occupied </strong>when kids on holidays. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子们一放假，我的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">行程就是满满的</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be overwhelmed  很忙乱</span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">if you had done what I asked you to do this morning, then I wouldn't have<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> been overwhelmed</strong> and I would have remembered my wallet.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">早上你要是按我说的做了，我就不会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得团团转</strong>，也不会把钱包落家里了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be crazy busy 忙疯了</span></strong></span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">been crazy busy</strong> these last few days!</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最近几天她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得不可开交</strong>！</p></section></section><section 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">口语</strong>|阅读|翻译|听写</p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hemi：前缀，表示half</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">spatial   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective  /ˈspeɪʃəl/   空间的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This task is designed to test children's spatial awareness </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这一任务是为测试孩子的空间意识而设计的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">neglect  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.疏忽，忽视；疏于照管</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Over the years the church has fallen into a state of neglect.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">多年来这座教堂已沦落到无人照管的地步。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 疏于照管；忽视，疏忽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He neglects that poor dog - he never takes him for walks or gives him any attention.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他对那只可怜的狗漠不关心——从不带它散步，也从不关心它。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">neglect to do sth：疏忽，疏漏，忘记做</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'd neglected to give him the name of the hotel where I'd be staying.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我忘了告诉他我住的宾馆的名字。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reveal    </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt.使显露；展现；显示</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A gap in the clouds revealed the Atlantic far below.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从云缝中可以看到远在下方的大西洋。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 揭露；泄露；透露</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was jailed for revealing secrets to the Russians.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他因为向俄国人泄密而被监禁。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. （电视节目最后的）揭示</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The final reveal of the new kitchen was a huge success.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最后大揭示的新厨房非常成功。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">distinction  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 区别，差别，不同; 卓越, 优秀, 盛名；荣誉, 殊荣, 奖赏</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I took grade five and got a distinction.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我参加了五级的考试并得了优良。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Consciousness  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 知觉，意识, 观念, 觉悟；察觉, 感觉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">national consciousness 民族意识；国族意识</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">conscious  是形容词：意识到；注意到；神志清醒的；有知觉的，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">常用的搭配是be conscious of (doing) something</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">subliminal  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj 下意识的；潜意识的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get to the bottom ofna.走到…的尽头；彻底查明(问题等) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">theologian</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美 [.θiə'loʊdʒən]  英 [.θiːə'ləʊdʒiən] n.神学家；神学研究者</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">theological</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美 [.θiə'lɑdʒɪk(ə)l]英 [.θiːə'lɒdʒɪk(ə)l]  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.神学(上)的；神学性质的；根据圣经的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">theology</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美 [θi'ɑlədʒi] 英 [θi'ɒlədʒi]    n.神学；宗教学；宗教信仰学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">consensus</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美 [kən'sensəs]英 [kən'sensəs]  n.一致的意见；共识</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sensory</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美 ['sensəri]  英 ['sensəri]  adj.感觉的；感官的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">disclose: 侧重指揭露或泄露鲜为人知或保密的事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">expose: 多指揭露丑闻、坏人坏事或各种阴谋。也可指某物暴露在外。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">uncover: 主要指移去遮盖物，让东西显露出来。也可指揭露阴谋、秘密等。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">distinction: 较正式用词，除指事物在本质上的差别外，还指在某一方面或某一细节上的区分，要在认真观察、研究后才易觉察。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">difference: 普通用词，可指事物本质上的差异或数量上的差额，也可指事物在某一方面的差别，还可指人们之间的不同意见。 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">discrepancy: 多用于言论和记述方面，指两物之间缺乏使之相似或平衡的协调。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">discrimination: 侧重指在判断、见识方面的差别，也可指待遇上的区别。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">aware: 强调通过耳闻目睹或感觉而得到的信息，也指敏税的观察和推断。侧重感知，多与of一起用。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">conscious: 指内心的感觉，强调深刻的心理活动。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sensible: 侧重通过直觉或理性感觉意识到某物的存在。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Tuesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">P.S.'s condition, known as hemispatial neglect,</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">P.S.</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">的病症叫做半侧空间忽略症，</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">reveals a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n im</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">portant distinction between the brain's processing <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of</em> information and our experience of tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> processing.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">它揭示了大脑处理信息和我们对于信息处理的经历的重要区别。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Tha</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t e</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">xperience is wha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> we call consciousness.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">这种经历我们称之为意识。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">We are conscious of both <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</em> external world and our internal selves</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我们对外在世界和自身内在有意识，</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">we are awa</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">re <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">an</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> image in much the same way we are awar</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of</em> </span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">ourselv</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">es looking a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t an i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">mage, or our inner thoughts and emotions.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我们意识到图像，和我们意识到自己在看图像的方式差不多，这与意识到我们内在的思想感情，基本是一样的。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">But where <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">does</em> consciousness come from?</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">但意识是从何而来呢？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Scientists, theologians, and philosophers have been trying to get to the bottom of this question for centuries— without reaching any consensus.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">科学家，神学家和哲学家们几个世纪以来一直致力于解决这个问题，但都没有达成共识。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">One recent theory is that consciousness is the brain's imperfect picture <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</em></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f</span></span></em><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;"> i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ts own activity.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">近来，有理论称意识是大脑对其自身活动的不完美写照。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">To understand this theory, it helps to have a clear idea of one important way the brain processes information from our senses.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">理解这个理论之前，我们先来理清大脑是怎么根据我们的感知来处理信息的。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Base</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">n sensory input, it builds models, which are continuously updating, simplifi</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> descriptions of objects and events in the world.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">大脑会根据我们的感官输入建立模型，这些模型不断地更新形成对于世间事物的简化描述。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We must now go back to Uncle Andrew. His poor old heart went pit-a-pat as he staggered down the attic stairs and he kept on dabbing at his forehead with a handkerchief. When he reached his bedroom, which was the floor below, he locked himself in. And the very first thing he did was to grope in his wardrobe for a bottle and a wine-glass which he always kept hidden there where Aunt Letty could not find them. He poured himself out a glassful of some nasty, grown-up drink and drank it off at one gulp. Then he drew a deep breath.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们有必要回头讲讲安德鲁舅舅。他从阁楼上跌跌绊绊地跑下去时，那颗可怜的老心脏砰砰地乱跳。他用手帕在额头上不断地揩着。当他进到楼下的卧室里，便把自己锁在毕面。他做的第一件事就是从衣柜里摸出一个瓶子和一个酒杯，他总是把这些东西藏在柜子里，以免被蕾蒂姨妈发现。他给自己满斟了一杯味道刺鼻的大人喝的酒，一口气喝了下去，然后，长长地舒了一口气。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你今天真的一定要工作吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是，恐怕是的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 可是你会错过足球赛的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 哦，那也没办法。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you really have to work today? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. I'm afraid so. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But you'll miss out on the football game. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh. Well, it can't be helped. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She buzzed around the kitchen making preparations for the party.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她在厨房里__________为这次聚会作准备。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">忙来忙去</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">realist 现实主义者；务实的人</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He’s an eternal <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">optimist</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他是个永远的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">乐观主义者</strong>。</p><p border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. adjust the sail(s) 调整风帆</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We can't direct the wind. But we can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">adjust the sail</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们不能控制风向，但我们可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">调整风帆</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sail既可作名词也可作动词</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6333333" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcd3jRzwd8JQ5h5X8fT7GyFk3GV9nDzYPic86BxEkibnm8pBm6pLypB9MS58kZnzmmPQib3yNMjHyYTA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="900" style="vertical-align:
