0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用 <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">expect XX to do XX </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Be based on/upon sth以...为基础</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：It is based on a true story.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它由真实故事改编。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Capture</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'kæptʃə/ US/'kæptʃɚ/(v.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">succeed in representing or expressing something intangible抓住...充分体现..</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：I mean, you captured it(get it). It's amazing.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我是说 你们抓住了精髓 棒极了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Appropriate </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ə'prəʊprɪət/ US/ə'proprɪət/(adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">suitable or acceptable for a particular situation恰当的，适当的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：But one day, you are gonna meet someone more... Appropriate.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">可有一天，你会和更适合你的人相遇</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(v.)take something for own use:占用，挪用</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：She appropriated my unread newspaper and never returned it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她擅自把我没看过的报纸拿去看,并且没有归还。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Visual </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'vɪʒjʊəl/ US/'vɪʒʊəl/(adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">of vision: relating to vision or sight视觉的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Vision </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'vɪʒ(ə)n/ US/'vɪʒən/(n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">eyesight，the ability to see视力</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：It was a very visual form of communication and entertainment.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种非常视觉化的交流和娱乐方式。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Code </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/kəʊd/ US/kod/(v.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">put something in code: to put a message or text into code编码、编译</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：How many people here actually have coded?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在座的有哪些人编过程？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Brightness </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'braɪtnɪs/ US/'braɪtnɪs/(n.) -ness  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the intensity of light reflected or emitted by something 亮光，亮度，明度（颜色）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The sun burst upon the crowded city in all its brightness.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">喷薄而出的太阳悬挂在这座拥挤的城市的上空，光芒四射。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Wavelength </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'weɪvleŋθ/ US/'wevlɛŋθ/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the distance between a part of a wave of energy such as light or sound and the next similar part. (光波、音波等的) 波长</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：UVA, UVB, and UVC are classified according to their wavelengths.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a波紫外线，b波紫外线，和c波紫外线是由它们的波长来区分的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(2)If two people are on the same wavelength, they share similar interests or opinions. 志趣相投</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Correspond </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/kɒrɪ'spɒnd/US/ˌkɔrə'spɑnd/(V.)  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If one thing corresponds to another, there is a close similarity or connection between them. You can also say that two things correspond. 相一致; 相对应</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：And this shape corresponds to an emergency beacon.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个形状刚好和一个紧急求助信号吻合。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Perception </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/pə'sepʃ(ə)n/ US/pɚ'sɛpʃən/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Perception is the recognition of things using your senses, especially the sense of sight. (尤指通过视觉的) 感知</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：It extends your perception as a human.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它扩展了你作为一个人的感知。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oversimplify </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˏəuvəˈsɪmplɪfaɪ/ US/ˏəuvəˈsɪmplɪfaɪ/(v .) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">simplify to an excessive degree过于简单</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：One should not oversimplify the situation.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们不应该将形势过于简单化。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Keep track of记录；与…保持联系</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Who keeps track of that sort of thing?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">谁会记那种事啊？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Configuration </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/kən,fɪgə'reɪʃ(ə)n/ US/kən,fɪɡjə'reʃən/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">arrangement of parts: the way the parts of something are arranged and fit together 布局，排列，构造</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">network configuration 网络结构；网路配置</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">system configuration 系统配置；系统结构</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Configure(v.) to set up, design, or arrange the parts of something for a specific purpose配置,设定,使成形,使具一定形式</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Individual </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪndɪ'vɪdjʊ(ə)l/ US/ˌɪndɪ'vɪdʒuəl/(adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">relating to one person or thing, rather than to a large group. 单个的，单独的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Loneliness is a purely subjective, individual experience.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孤独是一种纯粹的主观体验。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Injure </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'ɪndʒə/ US/'ɪndʒɚ/(v.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cause damage or affect negatively使受伤; 伤害</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The engine was forced onto its side injuring several people.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">引擎被撞到另一侧，事件造成多人受伤。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Shift from从...转移,移动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The wind shifted from east to west.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">风由东转向西。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Internal</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪn'tɜːn(ə)l/ US/ɪn'tɝnl/(adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">used to describe things that exist or happen inside a particular person, object, or place. 体内的; 内部的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">External </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪk'stɜːn(ə)l/ US/ɪk'stɝnl/ (adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">used to indicate that something is on the outside of a surface or body, or that it exists, happens, or comes from outside. 外部的; 外来的; 外在的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：potential enemies were everywhere, internal and external.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">国内外到处都潜伏着敌人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">extrinsic motivation 外在动机；外在激励</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">intrinsic motivation: 内在动机；内在激励</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center center;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: cover;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKc1T1BrrOMAFicKtIc4ydv8rUwwrJeKfruxGo4P17AUQbXdbRZiaEic0rQ8x4b1ImODksqibky6NL9dIQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg");overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;'><section style="height: 100%;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"> <img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKc1T1BrrOMAFicKtIc4ydv8rUwwrJeKfruxGo4P17AUQbXdbRZiaEic0rQ8x4b1ImODksqibky6NL9dIQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="200" style="width: 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">大脑也需要关于它自己的模型。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Fo</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r e</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">xample, the brain has the ability to pa</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ttention to specific objects an</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d e</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">vents.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">例如，大脑有注意具体事物的能力。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">It also controls tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> focus, shifting i</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> from one thing t</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">o a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">nother, internal an</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">d </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">external, according to our needs.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">它还会根据我们的需要来控制这种专注，从一个东西转移到另外一个，从内在到外在。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He poured out a second glass and drank it too; then he began to change his clothes. You have never seen such clothes, but I can remember them. He put on a very high, shiny, stiff collar of the sort that made you hold your chin up all the time. He put on a white waistcoat with a pattern on it and arranged his gold watch chain across the front. He put on his best frock-coat, the one he kept for weddings and funerals. He got out his best tall hat and polished it up. There was a vase of flowers (put there by Aunt Letty) on his dressing table; he took one and put it in his buttonhole. He took a clean handkerchief (a lovely one such as you couldn't buy today) out of the little lefthand drawer and put a few drops of scent on it. He took his eye-glass, with the thick black ribbon, and screwed it into his eye; then he looked at himself in the mirror.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">又倒了一杯喝下去后，他开始换衣服。你从未见过这样的衣服，但我还记得。他戴上一副硬邦邦的闪光的高领子，这种领子使你的下巴不得不长时间地昂着，又套上一件有图案的内背心，把金表链挂在前面。接着，他穿上婚丧仪式才用的最好的衣服，拿出最好的高筒礼帽拍打干净。他的梳妆桌上放着一瓶花（蕾蒂姨妈放的），他摘下一朵插在扣眼里，又从左边的小抽履里掏出一块手帕（很漂亮．现在难以买到），往上面洒了几滴香水。他将系着黑色粗绸带的眼镜戴上，然后，对着镜子观赏起来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我要投诉。你们寄给我的账单错了。况且，这也不是第一次了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 啊，我向您道歉，夫人。我们这里刚用了新电脑。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 难道你们不认为是时候让它们正常工作了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我完全同意。保证不会再发生这种事了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I have a complaint to make. The bill you sent me was incorrect. What's more, it isn't the first time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Well, I must apologize, madam. We have new computers here, you know.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Don't you think it's about time you got them working properly?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I agree entirely. I assure you it won't happen again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He will __________ and review the company's rules and regulations.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他将监督并审查该公司的规章制度。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">monitor</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: 英音：舌边爆破；美音：弹舌音+舌侧音；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. </strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">XX be half the battle  </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">...是完成某事的关键（最艰难阶段）；成功了一大半</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Just getting an interview is <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">half the battle</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">只要得到面试机会就等于<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">成功了一半</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Getting the audience to like you is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">half the battle</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">让观众喜欢你意味着<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">成功了一大半</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Coming up with the idea is only <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">half the battle</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">想出这个主意只是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">成功的一半</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's more than <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">half the battle</span></em></strong> right there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这就已经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">迈出一大步</strong>了。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: border-box;">情境解读</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 40 40 0%;align-self: stretch;height: auto;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 7px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-image: linear-gradient(-225deg, rgb(105, 234, 203) 0%, rgb(234, 204, 248) 48%, rgb(102, 84, 241) 100%);height: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(92, 107, 192);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Emily和好友Judith在聚会上看到了前卫设计师组合们穿着时尚亮眼，Judith主动上前夸赞两位设计师的衣着抢眼。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px 26px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 5px 15px;overflow: hidden;background-image: linear-gradient(-225deg, rgb(105, 234, 203) 0%, rgb(234, 204, 248) 48%, rgb(102, 84, 241) 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(92, 107, 192);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频中找到今天的主题表达了吗？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the one that sticks out like a sore thumb 像一只肿痛的大拇指一样明显</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1：</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If van Gogh <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stuck out like a sore thumb</strong>, Gauguin poked it in the eye of the Impressionist bigwigs.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果梵高<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">如一只格格不入的大拇指</strong>。高更则会把这个手指戳进印象派大师的眼睛里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You're going to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out like a sore thumb</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你们这样去肯定<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">立马被认出来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong> 本身就是“显眼；醒目；引人注意；突出”的意思</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They wrote the notice in big red letters so that it would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong>. 他们用红色大字写出通知，这样会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">显眼一些</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Some things actually do <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong>. 但有些东西的确<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">非常引人注意</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sore thumb</strong> 是肿痛的大拇指</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 50%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.3548387" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfVOd2A2fQpsTu134F3K6BK0mxE38E2vkDTxbWTficXr6R8UPwS5V1C2p2LNbgroglCQmI86ch3GFw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="248" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(92, 107, 192);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那么，跟肿痛的大拇指一样，那当然是非常显眼了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达可以用在褒义或者贬义的语境中，如果用在褒义语境中就可以翻译成：鹤立鸡群；靓丽抢眼...如果是用在贬义的语境中就可以翻译成：格格不入...</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: </strong>from Europe to the public.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他借助自己的画廊将来自欧洲的<strong style="box-sizing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Emily和好友Judith在聚会上看到了前卫设计师组合们穿着时尚亮眼，Judith主动上前夸赞两位设计师的衣着抢眼。<br style="box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(92, 107, 192);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频中找到今天的主题表达了吗？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the one that sticks out like a sore thumb 像一只肿痛的大拇指一样明显</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1：</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If van Gogh <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stuck out like a sore thumb</strong>, Gauguin poked it in the eye of the Impressionist bigwigs.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果梵高<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">如一只格格不入的大拇指</strong>。高更则会把这个手指戳进印象派大师的眼睛里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You're going to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out like a sore thumb</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你们这样去肯定<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">立马被认出来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong> 本身就是“显眼；醒目；引人注意；突出”的意思</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They wrote the notice in big red letters so that it would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong>. 他们用红色大字写出通知，这样会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">显眼一些</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Some things actually do <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stick out</strong>. 但有些东西的确<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">非常引人注意</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sore thumb</strong> 是肿痛的大拇指</p></section></section><section data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfVOd2A2fQpsTu134F3K6BK0mxE38E2vkDTxbWTficXr6R8UPwS5V1C2p2LNbgroglCQmI86ch3GFw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="248" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(92, 107, 192);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那么，跟肿痛的大拇指一样，那当然是非常显眼了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达可以用在褒义或者贬义的语境中，如果用在褒义语境中就可以翻译成：鹤立鸡群；靓丽抢眼...如果是用在贬义的语境中就可以翻译成：格格不入...</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px 10px 10px;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(223, 233, 243) 0%, white 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: rgb(105, 234, 203) 0%, rgb(234, 204, 248) 48%, rgb(102, 84, 241) 100%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">其它词链</strong></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: transparent;background-image: linear-gradient(to top, rgb(252, 197, 228) 0%, rgb(253, 163, 75) 15%, style="box-sizing: border-box;">avant-garde   (艺术；音乐或文学方面)思想前卫</strong></span></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His galleries introduce<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> avant-garde artists </strong>from Europe to the public.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他借助自己的画廊将来自欧洲的<strong style="box-sizing: 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Direct</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Adjective  /daɪˈrekt/ /dɪˈrekt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：going in a straight line towards somewhere or someone without stopping or changing direction直通的，直达的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a direct route/line</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直通的路径／线路</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：without anyone or anything else being involved or between直接的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She decided to take direct control of the project.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她决定直接管理这个项目。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：complete完全的，全部的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a direct contrast</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完全的对比</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：Someone who is direct says what they think in a very honest way without worrying about other people's opinions.直率的，坦率的，直接的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I like her open and direct manner.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我喜欢她坦率直接的态度。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Adverb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：in a straight line towards somewhere without stopping or</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> changing direction直线地；直达地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Does this bus go direct to the airport?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这路公共汽车直接去机场吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：without anyone or anything else being involved or between直接地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I intended to go direct to the manager with my complaint.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我打算直接向经理投诉。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Verb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to control or be in charge of an activity, organization, etc.管理，领导，指挥</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She directs a large charity.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她主管一家大型慈善机构。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to tell people the direction in which they must drive指挥交通</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There was a police officer directing the traffic.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有一位警察在指挥交通。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to be in charge of a film or play and tell the actors how to play their parts导演（电影或戏剧），执导</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He wanted to give up acting and start directing.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他想放弃表演转而开始导演。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to aim something in a particular direction朝着，指向</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Was that remark directed towards me?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这话是对我说的吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to tell someone how to get somewhere给…指路（或方向）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Could you direct me to the airport?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你能告诉我去机场的路吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to order someone, especially officially（尤指正式地）命令</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The judge directed the defendant to remain silent.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">法官命令被告保持安静。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Assess </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to judge or decide the amount, value, quality, or importance of something评价；评定；对…估价</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The insurers will need to assess the flood damage.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">保险公司需要对洪水造成的损失进行估定。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Estimate、assess 和 evaluate 三个和“评估”有关的单词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">threat</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /θret/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a suggestion that something unpleasant or violent will happen,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> especially if a particular action or order is not followed威胁，恐吓</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be under threat of sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to be in a situation where people are threatening you with something bad or unpleasant受到…的威胁</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She left the country under threat of arrest if she returned.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她离开了那个国家，并被警告说一旦返回就会被逮捕。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Construct </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb   /kənˈstrʌkt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to build something or put together different parts to form</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">something whole建造；构筑；构成，组成</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to construct a new bridge/building</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">建造新桥梁／大楼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /ˈkɒn.strʌkt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an idea or an imaginary situation构想；观念；编造，杜撰</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His reputation as an eccentric is largely a media construct.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他行为古怪的名声多半源于媒体的杜撰。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">conception</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /kənˈsep.ʃən/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an idea of what something or someone is like, or a basic</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> understanding of a situation or a principle观念；概念；见解；构想</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">People from different cultures have different conceptions of the world.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不同文化背景的人对世界持有不同的看法。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the process of a male and a female sex cell joining and causing a</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">baby to start to form受孕，怀孕</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">from the moment of conception</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从受孕的那一刻</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Metaphysical  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective  /ˌmet̬.əˈfɪz.ɪ.kəl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：relating to the part of philosophy that is about understanding</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">existence and knowledge 形而上学的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">subjective</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective    /səbˈdʒek.tɪv/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：influenced by or based on personal beliefs or feelings, rather</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">than based on facts主观的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">More specific and less subjective criteria should be used in selecting </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">people for promotion within the company.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">公司内部决定升职人选时，需要借助更具体、更客观的标准。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">MRI</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun   /ˌem.ɑːrˈaɪ/  magnetic resonance imaging  /mæɡˈnet.ɪk/  /ˈrez.ən.əns/ /ɪˈmɪdʒ.ɪŋ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义： </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a system for producing electronic pictures of the organs inside a person's</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> body, using radio waves and a strong magnetic field磁共振成像</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pinpoint </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb  /ˈpɪn.pɔɪnt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to find out or say the exact position in space or time of something准确指出，确定（位置或时间）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It is not possible to pinpoint precisely the time of death.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">准确地确定死亡时间是不可能的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to discover or describe the exact facts about something查明；准确描述</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Emergency workers at the site are still unable to pinpoint the cause of the explosion.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现场的急救人员仍然无法确定爆炸的原因。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a very small spot of something极小的点</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a pinpoint of light光点</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：very exact确切的，精确的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The computer will calculate your position with pinpoint accuracy.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">计算机能够精确地计算出你的位置。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sensory</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective   /ˈsen.sər.i/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：connected with the physical senses of touch, smell, taste, hearing, and sight感觉的；感官的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stimulus</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /ˈstɪm.jə.ləs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：something that causes growth or activity刺激（物），激励（物）；促进因素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Foreign investment has been a stimulus to the industry.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">外国投资促进了该产业的发展。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：something that causes part of the body to react（使身体部位产生反应的）刺激</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The tip of the tongue is sensitive to salt and sweet stimuli and the back of the tongue is sensitive to bitter stimuli.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">舌尖对糖和盐的刺激很敏感，而舌根则对苦味的刺激很敏感。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(31, 73, 125);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> th</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ll.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Instantly, as it seemed to Uncle Andrew, the Queen towered up to an even greater height. Fire flashed from her eyes: she flung out her arm with the same gesture and the same horrible-sounding words that had lately turned the palacegates of Charn to dust. But nothing happened except that Aunt Letty, thinking that those horrible words were meant to be ordinary English, said: "I thought as much. The woman is drunk. Drunk! She can't even speak clearly."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">刹那间，安德鲁舅舅觉得，那女王似乎向上一挺，变得更加高大。她眼中冒火，伸出手臂，做了一个在恰思将宫门捣成灰烬时同样的动作，口中念出灭绝咒。然而，什么事情也没有发生。蓄蒂姨妈想，那些可怕的话大概也是英语，她说：“我想得不错。这女人一定喝醉了。醉了！连话也说不清楚。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 请帮我个忙。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 什么事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你能帮我去邮局发一下这个吗？我跟医生约好了，没时间去邮局。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 当然。我也想请你去看医生时给我拿些感冒药。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'd like you to do me a favor.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can you mail this at the post office for me? I have to go to the doctor for an appointment and I don't have enough time to go to the post office.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sure. And I'd like you to get some cold medicine for me when you go to the doctor's.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She was knocked style="box-sizing: border-box;">When I walk along with two others, they may serve me as my teachers. I will select their good qualities and follow them, their bad qualities and avoid them. </strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(334.812px, 1273.73px);-webkit-transform: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;">walk中的字母l不发音；</span></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. avoid中的/v/的发音，要求上齿摩擦下唇，不要发成/w/。</strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);-moz-transform: 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：walk along with XX  </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和XX同行</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">May I <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">walk along with</span></strong></em> you? </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">与</strong>您<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">同行</strong>吗？</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：serve as XX  </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">履行XX义务；以XX为职业</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">served as</span></strong></em> a captain in the army.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他曾是一名陆军上尉。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I shall continue to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">serve as</span></em></strong> a trustee.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将继续<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">履行</strong>受托人的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">职责</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">serve as</span></em></strong> a resource teacher to all of the teachers.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我是所有老师的资源老师。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>It was a privilege to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">serve as</span></em></strong> a doctor.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">能够<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">作为</strong>一名医生<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为他人服务</strong>是一种荣幸。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">serve as</span></em></strong> treasurer to the union.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好吧，我<strong>是</strong>工会的财务主管。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1493.91px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1493.91px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 1493.91px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 1493.91px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKc6Z4Lz0afCSQfEgeMiaOn46oPRe3AgPg3U68KPia1nlW8tn9th4dgAziaS5fsL1OWwAMSlBKcicfEQ3A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《二流警探》</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Mace Tyrell will <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">serve as</span></em></strong> the second judge.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">梅斯·提利尔<strong>是</strong>第二法官。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1815.92px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1815.92px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 1815.92px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 1815.92px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6157407" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKc6Z4Lz0afCSQfEgeMiaOn46m0p0pHKwUrFSRCJvbefKXAXiaxTIlRCCfkyUX1N5kJKH9EKKVmpzI2A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《权力的游戏》</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 完整句子：</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I will select their good qualities and follow them,</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(I will select) their bad qualities and avoid them. </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">择其善者而从之，其不善者而改之。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. follow, avoid 含义相反</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">follow v. 跟着，跟随 → 从</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">avoid v. 避免，防止 → 改</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. quality n. 素质；品德，品性</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">good qualities 优点，好的方面；</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bad qualities 缺点，不好的方面</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Listening silently is a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">good quality</span></em></strong> that we should have.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">静静地倾听是我们应该具备的一种<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">好品质</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He has a lot of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">good qualities</span></em></strong> but being organized isn't one of them.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他有很多<strong style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">put up with sb/sth  忍受，忍耐</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> put up with</span> his violent temper.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">忍受</span></em>着他暴躁的脾气。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding:
