1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻白眼，先来看下中文释义：翻白眼是指黑眼珠偏斜，露出较多的眼白，是为难、失望、愤恨或不满时眼睛的表情。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“翻白眼”在电影中的表达非常形象生动：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">roll eyes</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">roll是一个及物动词，表示“卷起、翻起”。 </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">roll eyes字面意思是“翻起眼珠”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">即表达“对某些人或事的不屑一顾”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“白眼”本质上就是“给某人一个鄙视的眼神”<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还可以表达为：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">give somebody a disdainful look</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这里的disdainful是一个形容词</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">表示“轻蔑的、鄙视的”的意思</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最后这两个句子中，我们可以拓展学习一个句式：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> ...不是因为... 而是因为... </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He eats <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">because of </span>greed,<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> not</span> hunger.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">不是因为</span></em>饿了,<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">而是因为</span></em>贪嘴才吃的。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He failed in business <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">not because</span> <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">of</span> misfortune, <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">but because of </span>his own error.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他业务上的失败<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">不是由于</span></em>遇到了厄运,<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">而是由于</span></em>他自己的过错。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was through with sports, <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">not because</span> he had to be, <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">but because</span> he wanted it that way.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他放弃体育运动了，<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">不是因为</span></em>他非放弃不可，<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">而是因为</span></em>他想要那样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一般我们会按照正常顺序去翻译：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I won't tell him.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但是电影原文是这样：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He won't hear it from me.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">啥意思呢？至少我不会说出去。对方要是知道了，那也不是我说的（是别人说的）。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻白眼，先来看下中文释义：翻白眼是指黑眼珠偏斜，露出较多的眼白，是为难、失望、愤恨或不满时眼睛的表情。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“翻白眼”在电影中的表达非常形象生动：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">roll eyes</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">roll是一个及物动词，表示“卷起、翻起”。 </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">roll eyes字面意思是“翻起眼珠”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">即表达“对某些人或事的不屑一顾”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“白眼”本质上就是“给某人一个鄙视的眼神”<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还可以表达为：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">give somebody a disdainful look</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这里的disdainful是一个形容词</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">表示“轻蔑的、鄙视的”的意思</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The flames lit up the sky.火光照亮了天空。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">变得明亮</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Vegetative</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">&lt;adj&gt;植物的，植物性vegetative reproduction营养繁殖</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Line-方式，方法</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Line of argument/reasoning/inquiry辩论/推理/询问方法</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The police are following several different lines of enquiry.警方正在采用几种不同的调查方法。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were both thinking along the same lines.我们俩想法相同。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Inquiry </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɪnˈkwaɪəri $ ɪnˈkwaɪri/ &lt;n&gt;询问，打听</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We’re getting a lot of inquiries about our new London-Rio service.许多人来打听我们新开设的伦敦-里约热内卢的航班情况。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">调查，查究</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The police have launched a murder 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">随着我们利用科学解决意识的问题，我们将会开启关于人类特性的新探究。继续探索生命相关的重大问题，了解这个频道。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It must have been a terrible moment for the Witch when she suddenly realized that her power of turning people into dust, which had been quite real in her own world, was not going to work in ours. But she did not lose her nerve even for a second. Without wasting a thought on her disappointment, she lunged forward, caught Aunt Letty round the neck and the knees, raised her high above her head as if she had been no heavier than a doll, and threw her across the room. While Aunt Letty was still hurtling through the air, the housemaid (who was having a beautifully exciting morning) put her head in at the door and said, "If you please, sir, the ansom's come."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当女巫突然意识到，她那种能把人变成灰烬的魔力在她的世界里那么真实可行，而在我们这里却毫无用处时，对她来说这简直是个可怕的时刻。但她丝豪没有心慌意乱、沮丧失望。她扑向前，抓住蕾蒂姨妈的脖子和膝盖，将她高高地举过头顶，像举一个轻巧的玩具娃娃似的，朝屋子那头一甩。蕾蒂姨妈还没落地，女佣（她觉得那天早上真是妙不可言，令人激动）探头进来说：“先生，你的马车到了，请。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 各位，我提议大家为“年度最佳教师”玛丽·约翰逊敬一杯酒。她一整年辛勤工作，这份荣誉她当之无愧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对，我们都为她骄傲！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 敬你，玛丽！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 干杯！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Everybody, I'd like to propose a toast to Mary Johnson. Teacher of the Year. She worked hard all year. She really deserved the honor.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, we're all proud of her!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Here's to you, Mary!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Cheers!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a deal. I'll pick you up tomorrow morning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">____________。我明早来接你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一言为定</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>9.3 每日一句：</strong><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="text-align: justify;">Count me in.      </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: Knowing what you want is half the battle. Most people go through their whole lives not knowing what they want. It's easy to find if you know what you're looking for.  ">4. Knowing what you want is half the battle. Most people go through their whole lives not knowing what they want. It's easy to find if you know what you're looking for.  </a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be half the battle 的含义是？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 成功了一半   B 战斗的一半 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653554278&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=a9993c898c04df3732e415a79a0c9972&amp;chksm=f7ebc6abc09c4fbd7a22739db555babf8dbe64696ff57d444b336d0db398166f785c729d4f06&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. When I walk along with two others, they may serve me as my teachers. I will select their good qualities and follow them, their bad qualities and avoid them. ">5. When I walk along with two others, they may serve me as my teachers. When I walk along with two others, they may serve me as my teachers. I will select their good qualities and follow them, their bad qualities and avoid them. ">5. When I walk along with two others, they may serve me as my teachers. I will select their good qualities and follow them, their bad qualities and avoid them. </a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">qualities 的正确音标是：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> A /ˈkwɒləti/   <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">B /ˈkwɒlətiz/</strong>  C /ˈkwɒlətɪz/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(341px, 1831.5px);-webkit-transform: translate(341px, 1831.5px);-moz-transform: translate(341px, 1831.5px);-o-transform: translate(341px, 1831.5px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="height: 100%;width: 24px;float: right;border-bottom: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-right: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本文挖了几个空</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">试着填出来吧～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"lmpossible, I know. Not possible...(我知道不可能，绝对不可能…)</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...but it's happening."(但真的发生了)</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Okay.好吧</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Where am I?我在哪里？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">very clever.很妙嘛。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"The lake house."湖畔小屋。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The lake house. As you can see, l, too, am at the lake house...湖畔小屋好巧啊，我也在湖畔小屋。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...but I'm getting tired of these games so I'm leaving, okay? Bye.但我不想再玩这种游戏所以我要走了，再见。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Thank you. Bye.谢谢你，再见啰。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Maybe we should introduce ourselves properly.或许我们应该正式自我介绍。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1______________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">At least, trying to.至少在努力了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm an architect. I like to build.我是建筑师，我喜欢盖房子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And while I wouldn't say my current project is ideal...目前手边的案子虽然不尽理想。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...it allows me to be here, in this place, and that's enough for now.但至少让我来到此地目前这样就够了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But tell me something. If you're working in a hospital in Chicago now...请问一件事，目前你在芝加哥的医院上班，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...where were you before, in my time?那我这年代你在哪里？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Two years ago, in your time...两年前，在你的年代，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...I was working in internal medicine in Madison.我在麦迪逊当实习医生。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tell me about the future.告诉我未来的事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What's it like in the year 2006?2006年是怎样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm afraid the world's pretty much the same.世界应该没什么改变。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Of course, we all dress in shiny metal jump suits and drive flying cars...当然我们都穿太空衣开飞天车啦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...and no one talks anymore because we can read each other's minds.人与人都不说话因为我们会读心术。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But the truth is, man from the past...但事实上，来自过去的人…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...not much has really changed in 2006.2006年没太大的改变。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Speaking of the past, though, I've been thinking about the paw prints.提到过去，我一直在想脚印的事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How is that possible? -Well, I think we have the same dog.-怎么可能？-我们好像养了同一只狗。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, yeah? What's yours like?是吗？你的狗长怎样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">According to the vet, mine is eight years old in my time...兽医说我的狗八岁大在我的年代。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...six in yours.在你的年代是六岁。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2______________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't know why, but I call her Jack.不知为何，反正我叫他杰克。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hello, Jack.嗨，杰克。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width: 100%;line-height:
